			<font style="display: inline;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

		<p><font size="1"> </font></p><div style="width:100%">

			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>

		</p>

</div><hr size="3" style="color:#999999" width="100%" align="center"></hr><p style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p><div style="width:100%">

		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>

		</p>

</div>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt"><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">COVID-19 and Liquidity Update:</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Given the resurgence in COVID cases during the fourth quarter, the health and well-being of our employees and guests remains our top priority. We are benefitting from investments over the past several years including advanced air filtration systems, sanitizers throughout the restaurant, wellness protocols, and improved handwashing. In addition, we are closely following the recommendations of the CDC and local health departments and have implemented social distancing, wearing face masks, a tamper evident packaging seal for all digital orders, and created a new steward role to sanitize high-traffic areas. Collectively, these efforts give our employees and guests confidence that Chipotle remains steadfast in our commitment to keep them safe. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">As of December 31, 2020, Chipotle maintains a strong financial position with $1.1 billion in cash, investments and restricted cash, and no debt, along with a $600 million untapped credit facility with which to continue to navigate this crisis. Our financial strength gives us the opportunity to make on-going strategic investments in our people, business, and communities, which we believe will benefit us for years to come. At the same time, our team remains focused on reducing non-essential controllable costs and judiciously spending on return generating projects to preserve liquidity. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;">Fourth quarter 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;">20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;"> results:</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">Total r</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">evenue for the quarter was </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">$1.6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> billion, an increase of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">11.6%</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> from the fourth quarter of 201</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">9</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">. The increase in </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">total </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">revenue was driven by a </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">5.7%</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> increase in comparable restaurant sales and new restaurant openings. Comparable restaurant sales </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">were fairly consistent in each month of the fourth quarter due to a combination of factors including healthy demand for Carne Asada, strength in digital sales, and the benefit of a delivery menu price increase</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">Comparable restaurant sales began to improve towards the end of December and this trend has continued with January comparable restaurant sales growing around 11%. Comparable restaurant sales in the last week of January were in the high single digits, with winter weather across the country contributing to the lower comp. Assuming the pandemic doesn&#x2019;t worsen, we expect first quarter 2021 comparable restaurant sales to be in the mid to high teens range given an easier comparison during the second half of March.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Digital sales grew 177.2% year over year to $781.4 million and represented 49.0% of sales. About half of the digital sales were via delivery, benefiting from our expanded partnerships, with the remainder coming from order ahead transactions as guests better understand the value offered by this channel, as well as the convenience of more Chipotlanes.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">We opened </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">61</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> new restaurants including </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">two</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> relocation</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">s</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> during the quarter and closed </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">one</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">. &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">During the quarter, 42 of the 61 new restaurants </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">included </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">a</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> Chipotlane</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">. These formats continue to enhance customer access and convenience while also helping increase new restaurant sales, margins, and returns</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">. &nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">Food, beverage and packaging costs were </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">31.0%</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">total </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">revenue, a decrease of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">210</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> bps compared to the fourth quarter of 201</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">9</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">. The decrease was primarily due to the benefit of menu price increases</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">, along with better waste control and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">a more favorable</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> protein mix, partially offset by fewer sales of high margin beverages and higher dairy pricing</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">Restaurant level operating margin was 19.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">5</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">% in the quarter, an improvement from </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">19.2%</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> in the fourth quarter of 201</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">9</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">.&nbsp; The improvement was driven primarily by leverage from the comparable restaurant sales increase, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">menu price increases, and lower avocado pricing, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">partially offset by </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">COVID-19 related impacts including increased delivery expenses, exclusion pay and fewer sales of high margin beverages</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">. &nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">General and administrative expenses were&nbsp;$1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">24.0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> million&nbsp;on a GAAP basis, or&nbsp;$1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">14.4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> million</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-size:5pt;vertical-align:super;line-height:100%">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&nbsp;on a non-GAAP basis, excluding&nbsp;$6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">.8</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> million related to several legal matters and&nbsp;$2.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">8</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> million&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">related to transformation expenses, restaurant closure costs and certain other costs</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">. GAAP and non-GAAP general and administrative expenses for the fourth quarter of 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> also included underlying general and administrative expenses totaling</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> $89.6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> million,&nbsp;$2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">0.7</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> million&nbsp;related to non-cash stock compensation</font><a name="_Hlk62289715"></a><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">,&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">$0.5 million related to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">employer payroll taxes associated with equity awards</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">$</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">3.6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> million&nbsp;related to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">higher bonus accruals from our strong operating performance</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> despite the pandemic</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The GAAP effective tax rate was negative 62.2% in the fourth quarter of 2020, compared to 28.3% in the fourth quarter of 2019. The decrease was due primarily from our estimated federal net operating loss for tax year 2020, which we expect to carryback to the preceding five years. We generated a net operating loss for tax purposes due to several factors, including the impact of COVID, increased tax deductions for equity vesting and exercises, accelerated tax depreciation deductions and various tax planning initiatives. The income tax benefit generated is due to the difference in federal tax rates between 2020 and the years to which the federal net operating loss will be carried back to. On a non-GAAP basis, the 2020 fourth quarter effective tax rate was 24.6%</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;font-size:5pt;vertical-align:super;line-height:100%">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;font-size:5pt;vertical-align:super;line-height:100%">2</font><font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Non-GAAP general and administrative expenses </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">and non-GAAP effective tax rate are </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">non-GAAP measure</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">s</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. Reconciliations to GAAP measures and further information are set forth in the table at the end of this press release.</font>

</div>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt"><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Net income for the fourth quarter of 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> was </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$191.0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million, or </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$6.69</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> per diluted share, compared to net income of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$72.4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">or </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$2.55</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> per diluted share, in the fourth quarter of 201</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">9</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. Excluding the impact of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">the tax benefit described above, legal expenses, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">corporate restructuring, and certain other costs, adjusted net income was $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">99.3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million and adjusted diluted earnings per share was $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">3.48</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The adjusted diluted earnings per share was negatively impacted 3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> cents by several items due to the increased severity of the COVID-19 pandemic including exclusion pay and higher medical claims, as well as </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">9</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> cents from performance bonus accruals.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Full year 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;"> results</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">:</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Total r</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">evenue for 2020 was $6.0 billion, an increase of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">7.1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% from 2019. The increase in </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">total </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">revenue was driven by a 1.8% increase in comparable restaurant sales </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">and new restaurant openings.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Digital sales grew </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">174.1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% year over year to $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2.8</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">b</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">illion and represented 4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% of sales. About half of the digital sales were via delivery, benefiting from our expanded partnerships, with the remainder coming from order ahead transactions as guests better understand the value offered by this channel, as well as the convenience of more Chipotlanes.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">We opened 161 new restaurants during the year, including six relocations, and closed nine, bringing the total restaurant count at year-end to 2,768.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> Of the 161 new restaurants opened during the year, 100 (or 62%) included a Chipotlane. There are a total of 170 Chipotlanes as of year-end.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Food, beverage and packaging costs were 32.3% of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">total </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">revenue, a </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">decrease</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> of 80 bps compared to 201</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">9</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. The </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">decrease</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> was driven </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">by menu price increases taken in the second half of 2020, favorable avocado pricing and better waste control. These benefits were partially offset by fewer sales of high margin beverages, COVID-19 related menu mix shifts, elevated beef pricing due to industry supply interruptions in the summer, and higher dairy pricing. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Restaurant level operating margin was 1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">7</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% for </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2020</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, a</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> decrease</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> from </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">20.5</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% in </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2019</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. The </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">decrease</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> was </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">driven </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">primarily by COVID-19 related impacts including increased delivery</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> expenses</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">assistance and exclusion pay, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">elevated beef prices, increased incidence of steak, and fewer sales of high margin beverages. The decrease was partially offset by </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">benefits from menu price increases</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, lower avocado </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">pricing</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">improved labor efficiency realized from digital enhancements to the restaurants.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">General and administrative expenses were&nbsp;$466.3 million&nbsp;on a GAAP basis, or&nbsp;$</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">417.6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million&nbsp;on a non-GAAP basis, excluding&nbsp;$3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">5</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">5</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million related to several legal matters and&nbsp;$13.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million&nbsp;</font><a name="_Hlk62296036"></a><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">related to transformation expenses, restaurant closure costs and certain other costs</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. GAAP and non-GAAP general and administrative expenses for the full year also included underlying general and administrative expenses totaling&nbsp;$</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">32</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">6.4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million,&nbsp;$</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">78.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million&nbsp;related to non-cash stock compensation,&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$7.1 million related to employer payroll taxes associated with equity awards, $2.5M related to our All Manager&#x2019;s Conference, which was cancelled due to COVID-19,&nbsp;&nbsp;and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">3.6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million&nbsp;related to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">additional </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">bonus accruals from our strong operating performance</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> despite the pandemic</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;</font><a name="_Hlk505335379"></a>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The GAAP effective tax rate was </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">negative </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">21.1% in 2020, compared to 23.6% in 2019</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The decrease</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> was </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">primarily </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">due to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">the federal net operating loss that is estimated for tax year 2020, which we expect to carryback to the preceding five years. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">We generated a net operating loss for tax purposes due to several factors, including the impact of COVID, increased tax deductions for equity vesting and exercises, accelerated tax depreciation deductions and various tax planning initiatives. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The income tax benefit generated is due to the difference in federal tax rates between 2020 and the years that the federal net operating loss will be carried back to. On a non-GAAP basis, the 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> full year effective tax rate was </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">15.3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">%.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Net income for 2020 was $355.8 million, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">or $12.52 per diluted share, compared to net income of $350.2 million, or $12.38 per diluted share for 201</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">9</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. Excluding the impact of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">the tax benefit described above, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">legal expenses, corporate restructuring, restaurant asset impairment, and certain other costs, adjusted net income was $3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">05</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million and adjusted diluted earnings per share was $1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">73</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">More information will be available in our Annual Report on Form 10-K, which we expect to file with the SEC by February 9, 2021. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt"><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Definitions</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> following definitions apply to these terms as used throughout this release:</font>
		</p>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">

			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Comparable restaurant sales, or sales comps, and comparable restaurant transactions, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">represent the change in period-over-period total revenue or transactions for restaurants in operation for at least 13 full calendar months.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">

				<font style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Average restaurant sales </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">refer to the average trailing 12-month food and beverage revenue for restaurants in operation for at least 12 full calendar months.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Restaurant level operating margin</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> represents total revenue less direct restaurant operating costs, expressed as a percent of total revenue.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Digital sales</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> represent food and beverage revenue generated through the Chipotle website, Chipotle app or third-party delivery aggregators. Digital sales exclude revenue deferrals associated with Chipotle Rewards. </font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Chipotle</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">will</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> host a conference call to discuss fourth quarter and full year 2020 financial results on Tuesday, February 2, 2021, at 4:30 PM Eastern time.&nbsp; </font>

The call will be webcast live from the company's website on the investor relations page at ir.chipotle.com/events. An archived webcast will be available approximately one hour after the end of the call.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">About Chipotle</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Chipotle Mexican Grill, Inc. (NYSE: CMG) is cultivating a better world by serving responsibly sourced, classically-cooked, real food with wholesome ingredients without artificial colors, flavors or preservatives. Chipotle had over 2,750 restaurants as of December 31, 2020, in the United States, Canada, the United Kingdom, France and Germany and is the only restaurant company of its size that owns and operates all its restaurants. With nearly 88,000 employees passionate about providing a great guest experience, Chipotle is a longtime leader and innovator in the food industry. Chipotle is committed to making its food more accessible to everyone while continuing to be a brand with a demonstrated purpose as it leads the way in digital, technology and sustainable business practices. Steve Ells, founder, first opened Chipotle with a single restaurant in Denver, Colorado in 1993. For more information or to place an order online, visit </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#C08C19;background-color: #FFFFFF;">WWW.CHIPOTLE.COM</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

		</p>

		</p>

		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt"><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Forward-Looking Statements </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">Certain statements in this press release, including statements under the heading &#x201C;Outlook&#x201D; about our anticipated comparable restaurant sales, effective tax rate and estimated number of new restaurant openings in 2021, and projected comparable restaurant sales for the first quarter of 2021, are forward-looking statements as defined in the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. We use words such as &#x201C;anticipate&#x201D;, &#x201C;believe&#x201D;, &#x201C;could&#x201D;, &#x201C;should&#x201D;, &#x201C;estimate&#x201D;, &#x201C;expect&#x201D;, &#x201C;intend&#x201D;, &#x201C;project&#x201D;, &#x201C;target&#x201D;, and similar terms and phrases, including references to assumptions, to identify forward-looking statements. The forward-looking statements in this press release are based on currently available operating, financial and competitive information available to us as of the date of this release and we assume no obligation to update these forward-looking statements. These statements are subject to risks and uncertainties that could cause actual results to differ materially from those described in the statements, including but not limited to: the ongoing adverse effect of the novel coronavirus (COVID-19) pandemic on our guest traffic, restaurant sales and operating costs as a result of actions we have taken in response to the coronavirus, including closing some restaurants, ending dine in service at some restaurants while continuing to offer only takeout and/or delivery, modifying work hours at some restaurants, extending enhanced benefits to employees working during and/or impacted by the coronavirus, increasing compensation for restaurant employees, purchasing masks, gloves and additional sanitation supplies and services and delaying the construction of new restaurant openings; risks that the impact of the coronavirus pandemic will continue for a long duration and may require a more drastic response, such as closing all or most restaurants; risks of food safety and food-borne illnesses and other health concerns about our food; risks associated with our reliance on certain information technology systems and potential failures or interruptions; privacy and cyber security risks related to our acceptance of electronic payments or electronic processing of confidential customer or employee information; the impact of competition, including from sources outside the restaurant industry; the increasingly competitive labor market and our ability to attract and retain qualified employees; the impact of federal, state or local government regulations relating to our employees, employment practices, restaurant design and construction, and the sale of food or alcoholic beverages; our ability to achieve our planned growth, such as the availability of suitable new restaurant sites; increases in ingredient and other operating costs due to our Food With Integrity philosophy, tariffs or trade restrictions and supply shortages; the uncertainty of our ability to achieve expected levels of comparable restaurant sales due to factors such as changes in consumers' perceptions of our brand, including as a result of actual or rumored food safety concerns or other negative publicity, decreased overall consumer spending (including but not limited to the increase in unemployment caused by the coronavirus pandemic), or the inability to increase menu prices or realize the benefits of menu price increases; risks associated with our increased focus on our digital business, including risks arising from our reliance on third party delivery services, which are heightened during the pendency of government restrictions on dine in restaurant services as a result of the coronavirus pandemic; risks relating to litigation, including possible governmental actions related to food safety incidents and potential class action litigation regarding employment laws, advertising claims or other matters; and other risk factors described from time to time in our SEC reports, including our annual report on Form 10-K and quarterly reports on Form 10-Q, all of which are available on the investor relations page of our website at ir.Chipotle.com. </font>

			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">R</font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">ECONCILIATION OF NON-GAAP FINANCIAL MEASURES</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:10pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">The following </font><font style="display: inline;">table </font><font style="display: inline;">provides </font><font style="display: inline;">a reconciliation</font><font style="display: inline;"> of non-GAAP financial measures presented in </font><font style="display: inline;">the text above</font><font style="display: inline;"> to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:10pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">Adjusted net income is net income excluding </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">restaurant asset impairment, corporate restructuring, distinct legal proceedings, and certain other costs</font><font style="display: inline;">. Adjusted general and administrative expense is general and administrative expense excluding distinct legal proceedings, </font><font style="display: inline;">transformation expenses, restaurant closure costs and certain other costs</font><font style="display: inline;">. We present these non-GAAP measures in order to facilitate meaningful evaluation of our operating performance across periods. These adjustments are intended to provide greater transparency of underlying performance and to allow investors to evaluate our business on the same basis as our management, which uses these non-GAAP measures in evaluating the company&#x2019;s performance. Our adjusted net income, adjusted diluted earnings per share, and adjusted general and administrative expenses measures may not be comparable to other companies&#x2019; adjusted measures. These adjustments are not necessarily indicative of what our actual financial performance would have been during the periods presented and should be viewed in addition to, and not as an alternative to, our results prepared in accordance with GAAP. Further details regarding these adjustments are included in the tables below.</font>
		</p>

// Edgar(tm) Renderer was created by staff of the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission.  Data and content created by government employees within the scope of their employment are not subject to domestic copyright protection. 17 U.S.C. 105.
var Show={};Show.LastAR=null,Show.showAR=function(a,r,w){if(Show.LastAR)Show.hideAR();var e=a;while(e&&e.nodeName!='TABLE')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e||e.nodeName!='TABLE'){var ref=((window)?w.document:document).getElementById(r);if(ref){e=ref.cloneNode(!0);
e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
e.style.display=d;if(a.textContent){a.textContent=p+a.textContent.substring(1)}else{a.innerText=p+a.innerText.substring(1)}}}

}

}

	color: black;
